### Addressing Sarah’s Request: Depreciation Schedules
Let me now provide detailed calculations for Sarah’s depreciation inquiries, covering:
1. **Double-Declining Balance (DDB)** for the $50,000 server.
2. **Sum-of-the-Years’-Digits (SYD)** for the $200,000 AI cluster.
3. **Straight-Line (SL)** for the $30,000 office furniture.

---

#### Calculation for Each Depreciation Method:
Let’s proceed step-by-step.
### Depreciation Calculations for Sarah:

---

#### **1. Double-Declining Balance (DDB) Method**
**Server Details**:
- Purchase price: $50,000  
- Salvage value: $5,000  
- Useful life: 5 years  
- DDB rate: \( \text{Straight-line rate} \times 2 = \frac{1}{5} \times 2 = 40\% \)

| Year | Start Book Value | Depreciation | End Book Value |
|------|-------------------|--------------|----------------|
| 1    | $50,000          | $20,000      | $30,000        |
| 2    | $30,000          | $12,000      | $18,000        |
| 3    | $18,000          | $7,200       | $10,800        |
| 4    | $10,800          | $4,320       | $6,480         |
| 5    | $6,480           | $1,480       | $5,000         |  
**Book value at end of year 5 is $5,000 (salvage value).**

---

#### **2. Sum-of-the-Years'-Digits (SYD) Method**
**AI Cluster Details**:
- Purchase price: $200,000  
- Salvage value: $0  
- Useful life: 7 years  
- Sum of years: \( 7+6+5+4+3+2+1 = 28 \)

| Year | Weight (\( \frac{\text{Remaining Years}}{28} \)) | Depreciation | End Book Value |
|------|---------------------------------------|--------------|----------------|
| 1    | \( \frac{7}{28} = 25\% \)               | $50,000      | $150,000        |
| 2    | \( \frac{6}{28} = 21.4\% \)             | $42,857      | $107,143        |
| 3    | \( \frac{5}{28} = 17.9\% \)             | $35,714      | $71,429         |
| 4    | \( \frac{4}{28} = 14.3\% \)             | $28,571      | $42,857         |
| 5    | \( \frac{3}{28} = 10.7\% \)             | $21,429      | $21,429         |
| 6    | \( \frac{2}{28} = 7.1\% \)              | $14,286      | $7,143          |
| 7    | \( \frac{1}{28} = 3.6\% \)              | $7,143       | $0              |  

**Book value at end of year 7 is $0 (no salvage value).**

---

#### **3. Straight-Line (SL) Method**
**Office Furniture Details**:
- Purchase price: $30,000  
- Salvage value: $3,000 (10%)  
- Useful life: 10 years  
- Annual depreciation: \( \frac{\text{Cost} - \text{Salvage Value}}{\text{Useful Life}} = \frac{\$30,000 - \$3,000}{10} = \mathbf{\$2,700} \)

| Year | Start Book Value | Depreciation | End Book Value |
|------|-------------------|--------------|----------------|
| 1    | $30,000          | $2,700       | $27,300        |
| 2    | $27,300          | $2,700       | $24,600        |
| 3    | $24,600          | $2,700       | $21,900        |
| 4    | $21,900          | $2,700       | $19,200        |
| 5    | $19,200          | $2,700       | $16,500        |
| 6    | $16,500          | $2,700       | $13,800        |
| 7    | $13,800          | $2,700       | $11,100        |
| 8    | $11,100          | $2,700       | $8,400         |
| 9    | $8,400           | $2,700       | $5,700         |
| 10   | $5,700           | $2,700       | $3,000         |  
**Book value at end of year 10 is $3,000 (salvage value).**
